Driscoll<rod@theavitgroup.com.au>\r\n  -- Modified for other projects\r\n  -- Added Controls.SystemOnTrig (and Off) so other scripts can react when it is triggered\r\n  ]] --\r\n--------** Constant component\r\n\r\nMotionChoices = {\"Motion On/Off\", \"Motion Off\", \"Motion Disabled\"}\r\n\r\nMotionTimer = Timer.New() -- the additional timeout period after the motion sensor goes low\r\nGraceTimer = Timer.New() -- the timeout period after turning the system off where the motion sensor won't turn the system on\r\nWarmupTimer = Timer.New() -- the time it takes the system to warm up, power controls will lock out during this time.\r\nCooldownTimer = Timer.New() -- the time it takes the system to cool down, power controls will lock out during this time.\r\n\r\n--------** Functions **--------\r\n\r\n--------## Setup ##--------\r\nfunction Debug(str) -- helper function that prints debug statements when enabled\r\n    if Debugging then\r\n        print(\"[Debug] \" .. str)\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n--------## Notifications ##--------\r\n\r\nfunction PublishNotification()\r\n    SystemState = {\r\n      PowerState = Controls.SystemPower.Boolean,\r\n      SystemWarming = Controls.SystemWarming.Boolean,\r\n      SystemCooling = Controls.SystemCooling.Boolean,\r\n      AudioPrivacy = Controls.AudioPrivacy.Boolean,\r\n      VideoPrivacy = Controls.VideoPrivacy.Boolean,\r\n      VolumeLvl = Controls.VolumeFader.Position,\r\n      VolumeMute = Controls.VolumeMute.Boolean\r\n    }\r\n    Notifications.Publish(Controls.NotificationId.String, SystemState)\r\nend\r\n\r\n--------## System Components ##--------\r\n\r\nfunction GetComponentNames()\r\n    -- table to hold component names\r\n    local NamesTable = {\r\n        -- multi-dimensional table to store different component names\r\n        CallSyncNames = {}, -- call sync blocks\r\n        VideoBridgeNames = {}, -- video bridge blocks\r\n        DisplayNames = {}, -- display plugin blocks\r\n        GainNames = {}, -- gain blocks\r\n        MuteNames = {} -- system mute blocks\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    -- gather component names\r\n    for i, v in pairs(Component.GetComponents()) do\r\n        print(i, v.Name, v.Type)\r\n        if v.Type == \"call_sync\" then -- call sync\r\n            table.insert(NamesTable.CallSyncNames, v.Name)\r\n        elseif v.Type == \"usb_uvc\" then -- video bridge\r\n            table.insert(NamesTable.VideoBridgeNames, v.Name)\r\n        elseif v.Type == \"gain\" then -- call sync\r\n            table.insert(NamesTable.GainNames, v.Name)\r\n        elseif v.Type == \"system_mute\" then -- PSO Display Control Helper\r\n            table.insert(NamesTable.MuteNames, v.Name)\r\n        elseif v.Type == \"%PLUGIN%_78a74df3-40bf-447b-a714-f564ebae238a_%FP%_17f7c2b905c38a7cdf412359a2a9a848\" -- generic display plugin\r\n          or v.Type:lower():match('display') then\r\n            table.insert(NamesTable.DisplayNames, v.Name)\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\n\r\n    for i, v in pairs(NamesTable) do -- iterate through our tables of tables, format them for our combo boxes\r\n        table.sort(v) -- sort alphabetically\r\n        table.insert(v, ClearString) -- add \"[clear]\" to the end\r\n    end\r\n\r\n    -- set script choices\r\n    Controls.CallSyncComponent.Choices = NamesTable.CallSyncNames\r\n    Controls.VideoBridgeComponent.Choices = NamesTable.VideoBridgeNames\r\n\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Controls.DisplayComponents) do\r\n        v.Choices = NamesTable.DisplayNames\r\n    end\r\n\r\n    Controls.ProgramVolumeComponent.Choices = NamesTable.GainNames\r\n    Controls.SystemMuteComponent.Choices = NamesTable.MuteNames\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction CheckStatus()\r\n    for i, v in pairs(InvalidComponents) do\r\n        if v == true then -- we found\r\n            --Debug(\"There is at Least One Invalid Component\")\r\n            Controls.Status.String = \"Invalid Components\"\r\n            --Controls.Status.Value = 1\r\n            return\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\n    --Debug(\"No Invalid Components Found\")\r\n    Controls.Status.String = \"OK\"\r\n    Controls.Status.Value = 0\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetInvalidComponent(componentType)\r\n    InvalidComponents[componentType] = true\r\n    CheckStatus()\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetValidComponent(componentType)\r\n    InvalidComponents[componentType] = false\r\n    CheckStatus()\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetComponent(ctrl, componentType) -- a helper function that maps components to user selections\r\n    Debug(\"Setting Component: \" .. componentType)\r\n    componentName = ctrl.String\r\n    if componentName == \"\" then -- no component selected\r\n        Debug(\"No \" .. componentType .. \" Component Selected\")\r\n        ctrl.Color = \"white\"\r\n        SetValidComponent(componentType)\r\n        return nil\r\n    elseif componentName == ClearString then -- component has been cleared by the user\r\n        Debug(componentType .. \": Component Cleared\")\r\n        ctrl.String = \"\"\r\n        ctrl.Color = \"white\"\r\n        SetValidComponent(componentType)\r\n        return nil\r\n    elseif #Component.GetControls(Component.New(componentName)) < 1 then -- invalid component\r\n        Debug(componentType .. \" Component \" .. componentName .. \" is Invalid\")\r\n        ctrl.String = \"[Invalid Component Selected]\"\r\n        ctrl.Color = \"pink\"\r\n        SetInvalidComponent(componentType)\r\n        return nil\r\n    else -- great success!\r\n        Debug(\"Setting \" .. componentType .. \" Component: {\" .. ctrl.String .. \"}\")\r\n        ctrl.Color = \"white\"\r\n        SetValidComponent(componentType)\r\n        return Component.New(componentName)\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n---- Call Sync and Video Privacy ----\r\n\r\nfunction SetCallSyncComponent()\r\n    CallSync = SetComponent(Controls.CallSyncComponent, \"Call Sync\")\r\n    if CallSync ~= nil then -- success!\r\n        CallSync[\"off.hook\"].EventHandler = CallSyncCheckConnection -- attach event handler to system being in a call\r\n        CallSync[\"mute\"].EventHandler = CallSyncCheckMute -- attach event handler to call sync privacy\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction CallSyncCheckMute() -- helper function that sets the mute state of the call sync block\r\n    if CallSync ~= nil then\r\n        local state = CallSync[\"mute\"].Boolean\r\n        Debug(\"Call Sync Mute State is: \" .. tostring(state))\r\n        Controls.AudioPrivacy.Boolean = state\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetCallSyncMute(state) -- helper function that sets the mute state of the call sync block\r\n    if CallSync ~= nil then\r\n        Debug(\"Setting Call Sync Mute: \" .. tostring(state))\r\n        CallSync[\"mute\"].Boolean = state\r\n    end\r\n    Controls.AudioPrivacy.Boolean = state\r\n    PublishNotification()\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction CallSyncEnd(state) -- helper function that ends all calls using the call sync block\r\n    if CallSync ~= nil then\r\n        Debug(\"Ending Calls\")\r\n        CallSync[\"call.decline\"]:Trigger() -- end calls\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetVideoBridgeComponent()\r\n    VideoBridge = SetComponent(Controls.VideoBridgeComponent, \"Video Bridge\")\r\n    if VideoBridge ~= nil then -- success!\r\n        VideoBridge[\"toggle.privacy\"].EventHandler = GetVideoPrivacyState -- attach event handler to system being in a call\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction GetVideoPrivacyState()\r\n    if VideoBridge ~= nil then\r\n        local state = VideoBridge[\"toggle.privacy\"].Boolean\r\n        Debug(\"Video Privacy State is: \" .. tostring(state))\r\n        Controls.VideoPrivacy.Boolean = state\r\n        PublishNotification()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetVideoPrivacy(state)\r\n    if VideoBridge ~= nil then\r\n        Debug(\"Setting Video Privacy: \" .. tostring(state))\r\n        VideoBridge[\"toggle.privacy\"].Boolean = state\r\n    end\r\n    Controls.VideoPrivacy.Boolean = state\r\n    PublishNotification()\r\nend\r\n\r\n---- Displays ----\r\n\r\nfunction SetDisplayComponent(idx)\r\n    DisplayComponents[idx] = SetComponent(Controls.DisplayComponents[idx], \"Display [\" .. idx .. \"]\")\r\n    if DisplayComponents[idx] ~= nil then -- success!\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetDisplayOn(display)\r\n    if display[\"PowerOnTrigger\"] then -- check for valid component control\r\n        --Debug(\"Turning On Display\")\r\n        display[\"PowerOnTrigger\"]:Trigger()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetDisplayOff(display)\r\n    if display[\"PowerOffTrigger\"] then -- check for valid component control\r\n        --Debug(\"Turning Off Display\")\r\n        display[\"PowerOffTrigger\"]:Trigger()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetDisplayPower(state)\r\n    for i, v in pairs(DisplayComponents) do -- iterate through display components, using pairs because some might be nil\r\n        if state then\r\n            -- Debug(\"Turning Displays On\")\r\n            SetDisplayOn(v)\r\n        else\r\n            -- Debug(\"Turning Displays Off\")\r\n            SetDisplayOff(v)\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n---- Motion ----\r\n\r\nfunction CheckMotion()\r\n    Debug(\"Checking Motion\")\r\n    if Controls.MotionIn.Boolean then -- is there motion in the space?\r\n        Controls.MotionTimeoutActive.Boolean = false\r\n        MotionTimer:Stop() -- stop the motion timeout\r\n        if\r\n            not Controls.SystemPower.Boolean and not Controls.MotionGraceActive.Boolean and\r\n                Controls.MotionMode.String==\"Motion On/Off\"\r\n         then -- turn system on if the system is off, and motion on is enabled\r\n            Debug(\"Turning System on from Motion\")\r\n            SystemPowerOn()\r\n        end\r\n    else -- no motion in the space\r\n        if Controls.MotionMode.String==\"Motion On/Off\" or Controls.MotionMode.String==\"Motion Off\" then -- system off from no motion\r\n            Debug(\"Starting Motion Off Timer\")\r\n            Controls.MotionTimeoutActive.Boolean = true\r\n            MotionTimer:Start(Controls.MotionTimeout.Value) -- start motion timeout from user value\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n---- System Mute ----\r\n\r\nfunction SetMuteComponent()\r\n    SystemMute = SetComponent(Controls.SystemMuteComponent, \"System Mute\")\r\n    if SystemMute ~= nil then -- success!\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetSystemMute(state) -- mute all audio in the system using the system mute block\r\n    if SystemMute ~= nil then\r\n        --Debug(\"Setting System Mute\")\r\n        SystemMute[\"mute\"].Boolean = state\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n---- Volume ----\r\n\r\nfunction SetGainComponent()\r\n    ProgramVolume = SetComponent(Controls.ProgramVolumeComponent, \"Program Volume\")\r\n    if ProgramVolume ~= nil then -- success!\r\n        GetVolumeLvl()\r\n        GetVolumeMute()\r\n        ProgramVolume[\"gain\"].EventHandler = GetVolumeLvl\r\n        ProgramVolume[\"mute\"].EventHandler = GetVolumeMute\r\n\r\n        Controls.VolumeFader.EventHandler = SetVolumeLvl\r\n\r\n        Controls.VolumeMute.EventHandler = function(ctl)\r\n          SetVolumeMute(ctl.Boolean)\r\n        end \r\n\r\n        Controls.VolumeUpDown[1].EventHandler = function(ctl)\r\n            SetVolumeUpDown(\"stepper.increase\", ctl.Boolean)\r\n        end\r\n        \r\n        Controls.VolumeUpDown[2].EventHandler = function(ctl)\r\n            SetVolumeUpDown(\"stepper.decrease\", ctl.Boolean)\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetDefaultAudioLvl()\r\n    if ProgramVolume ~= nil and ProgramVolume[\"gain\"] ~= nil then\r\n        Debug(\"Setting Volume Percentage to: \" .. Controls.DefaultVolume.Position)\r\n        ProgramVolume[\"gain\"].Position = Controls.DefaultVolume.Position\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction GetVolumeLvl()\r\n    if ProgramVolume ~= nil then\r\n        Controls.VolumeFader.Position = ProgramVolume[\"gain\"].Position\r\n        PublishNotification()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction GetVolumeMute()\r\n    if ProgramVolume ~= nil then\r\n        Controls.VolumeMute.Boolean = ProgramVolume[\"mute\"].Boolean\r\n        PublishNotification()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetVolumeLvl()\r\n    if ProgramVolume ~= nil then\r\n        ProgramVolume[\"gain\"].Position = Controls.VolumeFader.Position\r\n        PublishNotification()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetVolumeMute(state)\r\n    if ProgramVolume ~= nil then\r\n        ProgramVolume[\"mute\"].Boolean = state\r\n        PublishNotification()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetVolumeUpDown(ctrl, state)\r\n    if ProgramVolume ~= nil then\r\n        ProgramVolume[ctrl].Boolean = state\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n--------## System Power ##--------\r\nfunction EnableDisablePowerControls(state)\r\n    Controls.SystemOnOff.IsDisabled = not state\r\n    Controls.SystemOn.IsDisabled = not state\r\n    Controls.SystemOnTrig.IsDisabled = not state\r\n    Controls.SystemOff.IsDisabled = not state\r\n    Controls.SystemOffTrig.IsDisabled = not state\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetSystemPowerFB(state)\r\n    Controls.SystemPower.Boolean = state -- update system power LED FB\r\n    Controls.SystemOnOff.Boolean = state -- update system power toggle FB\r\n    Controls.SystemOn.Boolean = state -- update system power on state trigger FB\r\n    Controls.SystemOnTrig.Boolean = state -- update system power on state trigger FB\r\n    Controls.SystemOff.Boolean = not state -- update system power off state trigger FB\r\n    Controls.SystemOffTrig.Boolean = not state -- update system power off state trigger FB\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SystemPowerOn(route) -- turn system on\r\n    Debug(\"Powering System On\")\r\n    Controls.SystemOnTrig:Trigger()\r\n    EnableDisablePowerControls(false) -- disable power controls\r\n    Controls.SystemWarming.Boolean = true -- system is warming\r\n    WarmupTimer:Start(Controls.WarmupTime.Value) -- start timer for warming fb\r\n    SetSystemPowerFB(true) -- update system power feedback\r\n    SetSystemMute(false) -- system mute off\r\n    SetDefaultAudioLvl() -- set system gain to default level\r\n    SetCallSyncMute(true) -- audio privacy on\r\n    SetVideoPrivacy(false) -- video privacy off\r\n    SetDisplayPower(true) -- turn dispays on\r\n    PublishNotification() -- send out notification with current system state\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SystemPowerOff() -- turn system off\r\n    Debug(\"Powering System Off\")\r\n    Controls.SystemOffTrig:Trigger()\r\n    EnableDisablePowerControls(false) -- disable power controls\r\n    Controls.SystemCooling.Boolean = true -- system is cooling\r\n    CooldownTimer:Start(Controls.CooldownTime.Value) -- start timer for cooling fb\r\n    SetSystemPowerFB(false) -- update system power feedback\r\n    SetSystemMute(true) -- system mute on\r\n    SetCallSyncMute(true) -- audio privacy on\r\n    SetVideoPrivacy(true) --video privacy on\r\n    SetDisplayPower(false) -- displays off\r\n    CallSyncEnd(false) -- send calls\r\n    PublishNotification() -- send out notification with current system state\r\nend\r\n\r\n-------- Fire Alarm --------\r\n\r\nfunction SetFireAlarm(state)\r\n    if state then -- fire alarm start\r\n        SetSystemMute(true) -- system mute on\r\n        SetDisplayPower(false) -- shut off displays\r\n    else -- fire alarm end\r\n        if Controls.SystemPower.Boolean then -- system was on, so\r\n            SetSystemMute(false) -- system mute off\r\n            SetDisplayPower(true) -- turn displays back on\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n-------- Event Handlers --------\r\n\r\nMotionTimer.EventHandler = function()\r\n    -- trigger system off after timeout period ends\r\n    Debug(\"Motion Timeout\")\r\n    Controls.MotionTimeoutActive.Boolean = false\r\n    MotionTimer:Stop()\r\n    SystemPowerOff()\r\nend\r\n\r\nGraceTimer.EventHandler = function()\r\n    -- allow system to power on from motion after grace period ends\r\n    Debug(\"Grace Period Has Ended\")\r\n    Controls.MotionGraceActive.Boolean = false\r\n    GraceTimer:Stop()\r\nend\r\n\r\nWarmupTimer.EventHandler = function()\r\n    --re-enable power buttons after warmup period ends\r\n    Debug(\"Warmup Period Has Ended\")\r\n    Controls.SystemWarming.Boolean = false\r\n    EnableDisablePowerControls(true)\r\n    WarmupTimer:Stop()\r\n    PublishNotification() -- publish notification of current system state\r\nend\r\n\r\nCooldownTimer.EventHandler = function()\r\n    --re-enable power buttons after cooldown period ends\r\n    Debug(\"Cooldown Period Has Ended\")\r\n    Controls.SystemCooling.Boolean = false\r\n    EnableDisablePowerControls(true)\r\n    CooldownTimer:Stop()\r\n    PublishNotification() -- publish notification of current system state\r\nend\r\n\r\nControls.SystemOnOff.EventHandler = function(ctl) -- event handler for on/off toggle\r\n    if ctl.Boolean then -- system on\r\n        SystemPowerOn()\r\n    else\r\n        SystemPowerOff()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nlocal function SetSystemPowerOff()\r\n    SystemPowerOff()\r\n    -- trigger system off\r\n    Controls.MotionGraceActive.Boolean = true -- enable grace period\r\n    GraceTimer:Start(Controls.MotionGracePeriod.Value) -- start grace timer\r\nend \r\n\r\nControls.SystemOff.EventHandler     = SetSystemPowerOff\r\nControls.SystemOffTrig.EventHandler = SetSystemPowerOff\r\n\r\nControls.SystemOn.EventHandler     = SystemPowerOn -- trigger system on\r\nControls.SystemOnTrig.EventHandler = SystemPowerOn \r\n\r\nControls.AudioPrivacy.EventHandler = function(ctl) -- set audio privacy to button state\r\n    SetCallSyncMute(ctl.Boolean)\r\nend\r\n\r\nControls.VideoPrivacy.EventHandler = function(ctl) -- set video privacy to button state\r\n    SetVideoPrivacy(ctl.Boolean)\r\nend\r\n\r\n-- change in control component selections\r\nControls.CallSyncComponent.EventHandler = SetCallSyncComponent\r\nControls.VideoBridgeComponent.EventHandler = SetVideoBridgeComponent\r\nControls.MotionIn.EventHandler = CheckMotion\r\nControls.SystemMuteComponent.EventHandler = SetMuteComponent\r\nControls.ProgramVolumeComponent.EventHandler = SetGainComponent\r\n\r\nfor i, v in ipairs(Controls.DisplayComponents) do\r\n    v.EventHandler = function()\r\n        SetDisplayComponent(i)\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n-------- Always Run --------\r\nfunction init()\r\n    EnableDisablePowerControls(true) --enable power controls\r\n    GetVideoPrivacyState() --sync video privacy fb\r\n    GetComponentNames() -- populate combo boxes for component selection with script names\r\n\r\n    Controls.MotionMode.Choices = MotionChoices -- fill in combo boxes with motion control options\r\n\r\n    -- set components with what's currently selected \r\n    SetCallSyncComponent() \r\n    SetVideoBridgeComponent()\r\n    SetGainComponent()\r\n    SetMuteComponent()\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Controls.DisplayComponents) do\r\n        SetDisplayComponent(i)\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\ninit()\r\n--[[\r\n  \r\nScript Copyright 2025 QSC\r\n\r\n--Permission is hereby granted, free of charge, to any person obtaining a copy of this software ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n\r\nfunction ConvertRanges(val, inMin, inMax, outMin, outMax)\r\n  if val < inMin or val > inMax then\r\n    print(\"ConvertRanges: input val: {0} not within valid range inMin:{1}, inMax: {2}\", val, inMin, inMax);\r\n  else\r\n    local inRange = inMax - inMin;\r\n    local outRange = outMax - outMin;\r\n    return ((val - inMin) * outRange) / inRange + outMin;\r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\n-- end Utility functions ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n     \r\n--[[ Displays ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n  Synch with a scrit for managing displays in the system\r\n]]--\r\nlocal displays\r\n\r\nif ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n]]--\r\nlocal timeRemaining = 0\r\n\r\n-- Current status of the power (\"off\", \"on\", \"powering on\", \"powering off\")\r\nlocal powerStatus = Controls.PowerStatus\r\n\r\nfunction SetPowerStatus(val)\r\n  print(\"current power: \"..val);\r\n  powerStatus.String = val\r\n  Controls.PowerOn.Boolean        = val == \"on\"\r\n  Controls.PowerOnFb.Boolean      = val == \"on\"\r\n  Controls.PowerToggle.Boolean    = val == \"on\"\r\n  Controls.PowerOff.Boolean       = val == \"off\"\r\n off\"\r\nend\r\nSetPowerStatus(powerStatus.String)\r\n\r\nlocal pendingStatus\r\nlocal snapshot\r\n\r\nfunction SeTimeRemainingStatus(duration)\r\n  timeRemaining = duration\r\n  Controls.RemainingSeconds.Value = timeRemaining\r\n  if powerStatus.String:find(\"on\") then\r\n    Controls.PercentRemaining.Value = 100 * (Controls.PowerOnSeconds.Value-timeRemaining) / Controls.PowerOnSeconds.Value\r\n  elseif powerStatus.String:find(\"off\") then\r\n    Controls.PercentRemaining.Value = 100 * timeRemaining / Controls.PowerOffSeconds.Value\r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\n-- Function to update timeRemaining asynchronously every second\r\nlocal function updateTimeRemaining(duration, callback)\r\n  SeTimeRemainingStatus(duration)\r\n  local function timerCallback()\r\n    if timeRemaining > 0 then\r\n      print(\"Time remaining: \" .. timeRemaining .. \" seconds\")\r\n      SeTimeRemainingStatus(timeRemaining - 1)\r\n      Timer.CallAfter(timerCallback, 1.0) -- Wait 1 second before next callback\r\n    else\r\n      callback()\r\n    end\r\n  end\r\n  timerCallback()\r\nend\r\n  \r\n-- Function to trigger PowerOn\r\nfunction PowerOn(param)\r\n  print('PowerOn('..(param or '')..')')\r\n  pendingStatus = \"on\"\r\n  if powerStatus.String ~= \"on\" and not powerStatus.String:find(\"^powering\") then\r\n    SetPowerStatus(\"powering on\")\r\n    if snapshot ~= nil and #Component.GetControls(snapshot) > 0 then \r\n      print('recall snapshot on')\r\n      snapshot['load.2']:Trigger() \r\n    else print('no system power snapshot found')\r\n    end\r\n    if displays ~= nil and #Component.GetControls(displays) > 0  and displays.PowerOn then \r\n      print('Powering on displays')\r\n      if param==nil or param~='audio' then displays.PowerOn:Trigger() end\r\n    end\r\n    print(\"Powering on the device...\")\r\n    updateTimeRemaining(Controls.PowerOnSeconds.Value, function()\r\n      SetPowerStatus(\"on\")\r\n      print(\"Device is now powered on.\")\r\n      if pendingStatus == \"on\" then\r\n        pendingStatus = nil\r\n        PowerOn(param)\r\n      elseif pendingStatus == \"off\" then\r\n        pendingStatus = nil\r\n        PowerOff(param)\r\n      end\r\n    end)\r\n  elseif powerStatus.String == \"powering off\" then\r\n    print(\"Powering off in progress. PowerOn will be triggered once completed.\")\r\n  else\r\n    print(\"Device is already on or powering.\")\r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\n-- Function to trigger PowerOff\r\nfunction PowerOff(param)\r\n  print('PowerOff('..(param or '')..')')\r\n  pendingStatus = \"off\"\r\n  if powerStatus.String ~= \"off\" and not powerStatus.String:find(\"^powering\") then\r\n    SetPowerStatus(\"powering off\")\r\n    if snapshot ~= nil and #Component.GetControls(snapshot) > 0 then \r\n      print('recall snapshot off')\r\n      snapshot['load.1']:Trigger()\r\n    end\r\n    if displays ~= nil and #Component.GetControls(displays) > 0 and displays.PowerOff then \r\n      print('Powering off displays')\r\n      if param==nil or param~='audio' then displays.PowerOff:Trigger() end\r\n    end\r\n    if camera ~= nil and #Component.GetControls(camera) > 0 and camera.PowerOff then \r\n      print('Cameras to privacy')\r\n      --if param==nil or param~='audio' then camera.PowerOff:Trigger() end\r\n    end\r\n    print(\"Powering off the device...\")\r\n    updateTimeRemaining(Controls.PowerOffSeconds.Value, function()\r\n      SetPowerStatus(\"off\")\r\n      print(\"Device is now powered off.\")\r\n      if pendingStatus == \"on\" then\r\n        pendingStatus = nil\r\n        PowerOn(param)\r\n      elseif pendingStatus == \"off\" then\r\n        pendingStatus = nil\r\n        PowerOff(param)\r\n      end\r\n    end)\r\n  elseif powerStatus.String == \"powering on\" then\r\n    print(\"Powering on in progress. PowerOff will be triggered once completed.\")\r\n  else\r\n    print(\"Device is already off or powering.\")\r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\nControls.PowerOn.EventHandler = function(ctl)\r\n  if ctl.Boolean then PowerOn() end\r\nend\r\n\r\nControls.PowerOff.EventHandler = function(ctl)\r\n  if ctl.Boolean then PowerOff() end\r\nend\r\n\r\nControls.PowerToggle.EventHandler = function(ctl)\r\n  if ctl.Boolean then PowerOn()\r\n  else                PowerOFf() end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction InitSystemPower()\r\n  if     powerStatus.String == \"powering on\"  then SetPowerStatus(\"on\")\r\n  elseif powerStatus.String == \"powering off\" then SetPowerStatus(\"off\") end\r\nend\r\nInitSystemPower()\r\n\r\n\r\nif #Controls.SystemPowerSnapshotComponentID.String == 0 then \r\n layers and their controls\r\nPopups = {\r\n    {Buttons = {Controls.BtnPower}, Layer = \"Power Confirm\", Transition = \"fade\"}\r\n}\r\n\r\n-- A table of buttons that will close all popups\r\nPopupCloseBtns = {Controls.BtnPowerOffNo, Controls.BtnPowerOffYes}\r\n\r\n-- A multi-dimensional table that handles page navigation\r\nLayers = {\r\n    {Buttons = {Controls.BtnCameras}, Layer = \"Cameras\", Header = \"\", Transition = \"fade\"},\r\n    {Buttons = {Controls.BtnHelp}, Layer = \"Help\", Header = \"\", Transition = \"fade\"},\r\n    {Buttons = {Controls.BtnHome}, Layer = \"Home\", Header = \"\", Transition = \"fade\"}\r\n}\r\n\r\n-- Global Variables --\r\nDefaultPage = 3 -- default to home\r\n\r\n-------- Functions --------\r\n\r\nfunction PopulateScriptLists()\r\n    ScriptsList = {}\r\n    for i, v in pairs(Component.GetComponents()) do\r\n        --print(i, v.Name, v.Type)\r\n        if v.Type == \"device_controller_script\" then -- ControlScript\r\n            table.insert(ScriptsList, v.Name)\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\n    Controls.RoomControlsScript.Choices = ScriptsList\r\n    Controls.TextHelperScript.Choices = ScriptsList\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetRoomControls(ctl)\r\n    local roomControlName = Controls.RoomControlsScript.String\r\n    RoomControls = Component.New(roomControlName)\r\n    if RoomControls[\"SystemPower\"] then -- valid room control helper\r\n        print(\"Room Control Script is: \" .. roomControlName)\r\n        SetSystemPower() -- always get current power state\r\n        RoomControls[\"SystemPower\"].EventHandler = SetSystemPower -- subscribe to updates in system power\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetTextHelper()\r\n    local textHelperName = Controls.TextHelperScript.String\r\n    TextHelper = Component.New(textHelperName)\r\n    if TextHelper[\"RoomName\"] then -- valid text helper\r\n        print(\"Text Helper Script is: \" .. textHelperName)\r\n        SetCurrentLanguage() -- always get current language\r\n        TextHelper[\"LanguageSelect\"].EventHandler = SetCurrentLanguage -- subscribe to updates in language\r\n        SetPowerText() -- always sync power off/on legends\r\n        TextHelper[\"ShutdownNo\"].EventHandler = SetPowerText -- subscribe to updates in language\r\n        TextHelper[\"ShutdownYes\"].EventHandler = SetPowerText -- subscribe to updates in language\r\n        for idx, _ in ipairs(Layers) do -- iterate through all of our primary layers\r\n            SetLayerHeader(idx) -- get the current header name for each layer\r\n            TextHelper[\"PageNames \" .. idx].EventHandler = function()\r\n                -- subscribe to updates in header text\r\n                SetLayerHeader(idx) -- update table with new text\r\n                if idx == CurrentPage then\r\n                    Controls.TxtHeader.String = Layers[CurrentPage].Header or \"\" -- make sure the header is updated to current text\r\n                end\r\n            end\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetCurrentLanguage()\r\n    if TextHelper then\r\n        CurrentLanguage = TextHelper[\"LanguageSelect\"].String\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetPowerText()\r\n    if TextHelper then\r\n        Controls.BtnPowerOffNo.Legend = TextHelper[\"ShutdownNo\"].String\r\n        Controls.BtnPowerOffYes.Legend = TextHelper[\"ShutdownYes\"].String\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetLayerHeader(page)\r\n    if Layers[page] and TextHelper then -- item exists and system text isn't null\r\n        Layers[page][\"Header\"] = TextHelper[\"PageNames \" .. page].String\r\n    --print(\"Page [\"..page..\"]: \" ..Layers[page][\"Header\"])\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetSystemPower() -- evaluates current system state and updates UCI state\r\n    if not RoomControls then\r\n        print(\"No Valid Room Controls\")\r\n        return\r\n    end\r\n    ClosePopups()\r\n    local state = RoomControls[\"SystemPower\"].Boolean\r\n    Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", \"Splash\", not state, \"none\")\r\n\r\n    if state then\r\n        ShowLayer(DefaultPage)\r\n    else\r\n        CloseLayers()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction ShowPopup(popup) -- show a specfic popup\r\n    ClosePopups() -- first, close all of the other popups for a clean look (this also closes all of the popups bgs)\r\n    --print(\"Showing Popup #: \".. popup)\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Popups) do -- iterate through all popups\r\n        Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", v.Layer, i == popup, v.Transition) -- show popup\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction ClosePopups() -- close all popups\r\n    --print(\"Hiding Popups\")\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Popups) do --iterate through all popups\r\n        Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", v.Layer, false, v.Transition) -- hide popup page\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction ShowLayer(nav) -- show a specfic page layer\r\n    CurrentPage = nav\r\n    ClosePopups() -- close all popups for a clean look\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Layers) do --iterate through Layers table\r\n        Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", v.Layer, i == nav, v.Transition) -- show/hide Layers\r\n        for i2, v2 in ipairs(v.Buttons) do --iterate through associated buttons\r\n            v2.Boolean = i == nav -- feedback for buttons\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\n    Controls.TxtHeader.String = Layers[CurrentPage].Header\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction CloseLayers() -- close all page layers\r\n    ClosePopups() -- close all popups for a clean look\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Layers) do --iterate through Layers table\r\n        Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", v.Layer, false, v.Transition) -- hide all Layers\r\n        for i2, v2 in ipairs(v.Buttons) do --iterate through associated buttons\r\n            v2.Boolean = false -- feedback low for all buttons\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n-------- Event Handlers --------\r\n\r\nfor idx, v in ipairs(Layers) do\r\n    for _, button in ipairs(v[\"Buttons\"]) do\r\n        button.EventHandler = function()\r\n            ShowLayer(idx)\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfor idx, v in ipairs(Popups) do\r\n    for _, button in ipairs(v[\"Buttons\"]) do\r\n        button.EventHandler = function()\r\n            ShowPopup(idx)\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfor _, button in ipairs(PopupCloseBtns) do\r\n    button.EventHandler = ClosePopups\r\nend\r\n\r\nControls.RoomControlsScript.EventHandler = SetRoomControls\r\nControls.TextHelperScript.EventHandler = SetTextHelper\r\n\r\n-------- Always Run --------\r\n\r\nfunction init()\r\n    PopulateScriptLists()\r\n    SetRoomControls()\r\n    SetTextHelper()\r\nend\r\n\r\ninit()\r\n\r\n--[[\r\n  \r\nScript Copyright 2025 QSC\r\n\r\n--Permission is Functions --------\r\n\r\n-- Notifications\r\n\r\nfunction RoomControlsSubscribe() -- subscribe for updates from the selected room\r\n  RoomControlsNotificationId = Controls.RoomControlsId.String or \"\"\r\n    if PanelTxtNoteId ~= nil then -- there is an existing subscription\r\n         Notifications.Unsubscribe(PanelTxtNoteId)\r\n    end\r\n    RoomControlsNoteId = Notifications.Subscribe(RoomControlsNotificationId, RoomControlsNotificationHandler)\r\n    print(\"System Status Subscription: \" .. tostring(PanelTxtNoteId))\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction PanelTxtSubscribe() -- subscribe for updates from the selected room\r\n  PanelTxtNotificationId = Controls.TextHelperId.String or \"\"\r\n    if PanelTxtNoteId ~= nil then -- there is an existing Text Subscription: \" .. tostring(PanelTxtNoteId))\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction RoomControlsNotificationHandler(name, note)\r\n    --print(\"System Status Announcement Received\")\r\n    RoomControls = note or {}\r\n    SetSystemPower()\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction PanelTxtNotificationHandler(name, note)\r\n    print(\"Panel Text Announcement Received\")\r\n    PanelText = note or {}\r\n    if PanelText then\r\n        CurrentLanguage = PanelText[\"LanguageSelect\"] or \"\"\r\n        Controls.BtnPowerOffNo.Legend = PanelText[\"ShutdownNo\"] or \"\"\r\n        Controls.BtnPowerOffYes.Legend = PanelText[\"ShutdownYes\"] or \"\"\r\n        for idx, layer in ipairs (Layers) do \r\n          layer[\"Header\"] = PanelText[\"PageNames\"][idx] \r\n        end\r\n    end\r\n      if CurrentPage and Layers[CurrentPage] then \r\n        Controls.TxtHeader.String = Layers[CurrentPage].Header or \"\"\r\n      end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SetSystemPower() -- evaluates current system state and updates UCI state\r\n    ClosePopups()\r\n    local state = RoomControls[\"PowerState\"] or false\r\n    Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", \"Splash\", not state, \"none\")\r\n\r\n    if state then\r\n        ShowLayer(DefaultPage)\r\n    else\r\n        CloseLayers()\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction ShowPopup(popup) -- show a specfic popup\r\n    ClosePopups() -- first, close all of the other popups for a clean look (this also closes all of the popups bgs)\r\n    --print(\"Showing Popup #: \".. popup)\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Popups) do -- iterate through all popups\r\n        Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", v.Layer, i == popup, v.Transition) -- show popup\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction ClosePopups() -- close all popups\r\n    --print(\"Hiding Popups\")\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Popups) do --iterate through all popups\r\n        Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", v.Layer, false, v.Transition) -- hide popup page\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction ShowLayer(nav) -- show a specfic page layer\r\n    CurrentPage = nav\r\n    ClosePopups() -- close all popups for a clean look\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Layers) do --iterate through Layers table\r\n        Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", v.Layer, i == nav, v.Transition) -- show/hide Layers\r\n        for i2, v2 in ipairs(v.Buttons) do --iterate through associated buttons\r\n            v2.Boolean = i == nav -- feedback for buttons\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\n    Controls.TxtHeader.String = Layers[CurrentPage].Header\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction CloseLayers() -- close all page layers\r\n    ClosePopups() -- close all popups for a clean look\r\n    for i, v in ipairs(Layers) do --iterate through Layers table\r\n        Uci.SetLayerVisibility(\"Main\", v.Layer, false, v.Transition) -- hide all Layers\r\n        for i2, v2 in ipairs(v.Buttons) do --iterate through associated buttons\r\n            v2.Boolean = false -- feedback low for all buttons\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n-------- Event Handlers --------\r\n\r\nfor idx, v in ipairs(Layers) do\r\n    for _, button in ipairs(v[\"Buttons\"]) do\r\n        button.EventHandler = function()\r\n            ShowLayer(idx)\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfor idx, v in ipairs(Popups) do\r\n    for _, button in ipairs(v[\"Buttons\"]) do\r\n        button.EventHandler = function()\r\n            ShowPopup(idx)\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfor _, button in ipairs(PopupCloseBtns) do\r\n    button.EventHandler = ClosePopups\r\nend\r\n\r\nControls.RoomControlsId.EventHandler = RoomControlsSubscribe\r\nControls.TextHelperId.EventHandler = PanelTxtNotificationId\r\n\r\n-- Always Run\r\nRoomControlsSubscribe()\r\nPanelTxtSubscribe()\r\n\r\n--[[\r\n  \r\nScript Copyright 2025 and pinEntered..val or val\r\n  print('pin entered '..pinEntered)\r\n  \r\n  if #pinEntered == 4 then\r\n    -- store\r\n    if pinStoreMode then \r\n      print('storing new user PIN')\r\n      room.RoomPIN.String = pinEntered\r\n      SetPINStoreMode(false)\r\n      ShowModal(false, 'PIN')\r\n    -- comparing\r\n    else\r\n      if pinEntered == backdoorPIN or pinEntered == -------------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n\r\n------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n-- modal\r\n------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n--The modal layer is shared amongst several functions\r\n\r\nlocal modalLayers = {}\r\n\r\nfunction addStringToTable(tbl, str)\r\n    for _, value in ipairs(tbl) do\r\n        if value == str then return end -- String already exists, so exit the function\r\n    end\r\n    table.insert(tbl, str) -- Add the string if it does not exist\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction removeStringFromTable(tbl, str)\r\n    for i, value in ipairs(tbl) do\r\n        if value == str then\r\n            table.remove(tbl, i) -- Remove the string from the table\r\n            return -- Exit the function once the string is removed\r\n        end\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction CloseModal(layer)\r\n    print('closing modal: '..layer)\r\n    removeStringFromTable(modalLayers, layer)\r\n    Uci.SetLayerVisibility(MainPage, layer, false, 'none')\r\nend \r\n\r\nfunction ShowModal(state, layer)\r\n  if state then -- adding\r\n    if layer then \r\n      addStringToTable(modalLayers, layer)\r\n      Uci.SetLayerVisibility(MainPage, layer, state, 'none')\r\n      Controls.btnModalClose.IsInvisible = layer == 'PIN'\r\n    end\r\n  else -- removing\r\n    if layer then CloseModal(layer) \r\n    else -- remove all\r\n      print('closing all modals')\r\n      for _, value in ipairs(modalLayers) do CloseModal(value) end\r\n    end\r\n  end\r\n    Uci.SetLayerVisibility(MainPage, 'Modal', #modalLayers > 0, 'none') \r\nend \r\n\r\nfunction InitModal()\r\n  Controls.btnModalClose.EventHandler = function(ctl)\r\n    if ctl.Type=='Trigger' or not ctl.Boolean then ShowModal(false) end\r\n  end\r\nend\r\nInitModal()\r\n-- End Modal ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n  Volume controls\r\n  This could be hard coded but managing it here enables us to change which level control to inMax, outMin, outMax)\r\n  if val < inMin or val > inMax then\r\n    print(\"ConvertRanges: input val: {0} not within valid range inMin:{1}, inMax: {2}\", val, inMin, inMax);\r\n  else\r\n    local inRange = inMax - inMin;\r\n    local outRange = outMax - outMin;\r\n    return ((val - inMin) * outRange) / inRange + outMin;\r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction UpdateMicMuteStatus()  \r\n  local muted_ then\r\n      if MicGainComponent.mute.Boolean then \r\n        print('['..i..'] true')\r\n        muted_ = true \r\n        break\r\n      end\r\n    else break\r\n    end\r\n  end\r\n  Controls.btnMicMute.Boolean = muted_ \r\n  Controls.btnMicMute.CssClass = 'sg-'..footerTone..(muted_ and '-mic-muted' or '-mic-mute')\r\nend  \r\n\r\nfunction InitMics()\r\n  print('Initialising (src_ and src_ or ''))\r\n    matrix['Selectors '..dest].String = src_ and src_ or ''\r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SourceSelect(left, right)\r\n  if leftOutput and left then \r\n    currentSource[leftOutput] = left  ~= currentSource[leftOutput] and left or 0\r\n    print('SourceSelect('..left..')['..currentSource[leftOutput]..'] '..sources[currentSource[leftOutput]].name)\r\n  end\r\n  if rightOutput and right then \r\n    currentSource[rightOutput] = right  ~= currentSource[rightOutput] and right or 0\r\n    print('SourceSelect(right: '..right..')['..currentSource[rightOutput]..'] '..sources[currentSource[rightOutput]].name)\r\n  end  \r\n  for i,_ in ipairs(sources) do\r\n    if Controls['btnControl_'..i] then Controls['btnControl_'..i].Boolean = currentSource[1] == i end\r\n    if currentSource[1] == i then\r\n      if leftOutput  and left  then RouteVideo(currentSource[leftOutput ], leftOutput) end\r\n      if rightOutput and right then RouteVideo(currentSource[rightOutput], rightOutput) end\r\n      if OverflowOutputs and Controls.btnZone2 and Controls.btnZone2.Boolean then\r\n        for _,v1 in ipairs(OverflowOutputs) do\r\n          RouteVideo(currentSource[leftOutput], v1)\r\n        end\r\n      end\r\n    end\r\n  end\r\n  if Controls.btnMTR then Controls.btnMTR.Boolean = currentSource[1] == MTRSources[1] end\r\n\r\n  if room.PowerStatus.String == 'on' and currentSource[1]>0 then \r\n    Controls.lblRoomStatus.String = 'Presenting ' .. sources[currentSource[1]].name\r\n  else\r\n    Controls.lblRoomStatus.String = \"System is \" .. room.PowerStatus.String\r\n  end\r\n  if currentSource[1]>0 and not room.PowerOnFb.Boolean then\r\n    room.PowerOn.Boolean = true \r\n  end\r\n  if displays and #Component.GetControls(displays) > 0 then\r\n    local power_ = displays['PowerO'..(currentSource[1]>0 and 'n' or 'ff')]:Trigger()\r\n  end\r\n\r\n  local IsInvisible_ = currentSource[1]==0 or not sources[currentSource[1]].name:match('Television')\r\n  Controls.lblTvChannel.IsInvisible = IsInvisible_\r\n  Controls.btnTvChannel.IsInvisible = IsInvisible_\r\n\r\n  IsInvisible_ = currentSource[1]==0 or not sources[currentSource[1]].name:match('^MTR')\r\n  if Controls.lblContent then\r\n Controls.btnCamera.IsInvisible = IsInvisible_\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction SharingSourceSelect(sharingSource)\r\n  local source = sharingSources[sharingSource].source\r\n  print('SharingSourceSelect('..sharingSource..'): ['..source..'] '..sources[source].name)\r\n  currentSharingSource = source ~= currentSharingSource and source or 0\r\n  local matrix = encoder: '..matrix[outputID].Choices[currentSharingSource+1])\r\n      matrix[outputID].String = matrix[outputID].Choices[currentSharingSource+1] -- first is blank\r\n    end\r\n  end\r\n sources[currentSource[1]].name..' - sharing '..sources[currentSharingSource].name\r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction ShowContentSub()\r\n  Controls.lblModal.String = \"Content sharing\"\r\n end\r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\nlocal function hangupCall() -- ctl+shift+h ** this only works if the MTR UI has focus, i.e if you can tab through buttons on the UI **\r\n  if HIDKeyboardComponent['key.left.shift'] then\r\n    print('hangupCall()')\r\n    HIDKeyboardComponent['key.left.shift'].Boolean = true\r\n    HIDKeyboardComponent['key.left.ctrl'].Boolean = true\r\n Uci.SetLayerVisibility(MainPage, 'Mode selection', sysMode < 1, 'none')\r\n  Uci.SetLayerVisibility(MainPage, 'Main'          , sysMode > 0, 'none')\r\n  ]]              \r\n UpdateRoomPower() \r\n  if room.PowerStatus.String == 'on' and currentSource[1]>0 then \r\n    Controls.lblRoomStatus.String = 'Presenting ' .. sources[currentSource[1]].name\r\n  else\r\n    Controls.lblRoomStatus.String = \"System is \" .. room.PowerStatus.String\r\n  end\r\n  print(\"current power: \"..Controls.lblRoomStatus.String);\r\n  Controls.lblNotification.Color = 'green'\r\n  Controls.btnPower.Boolean = room.PowerOnFb.Boolean\r\n  Controls.lblPower.Legend = 'power\\n'..room.PowerStatus.String\r\n\tUci.SetLayerVisibility(MainPage, 'Notification bar',\r\n                        room.PowerWarmingFb.Boolean or room.PowerCoolingFb.Boolean, \r\n                        'none')\r\n                        \r\n  if room.PowerStatus.String:find(\"off\") then SetSystemMode(0) --print('found off')\r\n  elseif sysMode == 0                    then SetSystemMode(1)\r\n  else                                        SetSystemMode(sysMode) end\r\n\r\n  BTMuteComponent = Component.New('BT gain')\r\n  if room.PowerOffFb.Boolean then \r\n    print('power off Fb')\r\n    SourceSelect(0,0)  \r\n    \r\n    if #Component.GetComponents(BTMuteComponent) > 0 then \r\n      print('muting Bluetooth with system power off')\r\n      if BTMuteComponent.mute then BTMuteComponent.mute.Boolean = true end\r\n    end\r\n    \r\n    CombineComponent = Component.New('Combine')\r\n    if #Component.GetControls(CombineComponent)>0 then\r\n      print('disabling combine with system power off')\r\n      if CombineComponent.mute then CombineComponent.mute.Boolean = true end\r\n    end\r\n\r\n    CameraSelect(1) -- this will stop the preview timer\r\n    hangupCall()\r\n  end\r\n  if room.PowerOnFb.Boolean \r\n    and currentSource[1]==0 \r\n    --and BTMuteComponent.mute.Boolean \r\n    and Controls.btnMTR\r\n    then SourceSelect(MTRSources[1], MTRSources[2]) \r\n  end\r\nend\r\n\r\nfunction InitRoomLabel()\r\n  --print(\"comp
